# 기로 원문 로그

**RiskyDice:** Automated welcome message
Thanks for updating the Item Macro
<p class="nue">Hello, I am Forien and with Kekilla's permission I took this module over
from him. My job here is mostly to keep this module maintained and working on Foundry v11
and future updates. That said I am not opposed to expanding this module with additional
systems or new features if there is big demand enough.</p> <p class="nue">Since I took
this module with next to no knowledge, keep in mind that I might not know if something is
broken or not working as intended. Please feel free to contact me on Foundry Discord by
pinging Forien. You can also join <a href="https://discord.gg/XkTFv8DRDc"
target="_blank">my Discord</a> or report an <a href="https://github.com/Foundry-
Workshop/Item-Macro/issues" target="_blank"> Issue on GitHub</a>.</p> <p class="nue">I'm
creating Foundry modules (full list of which you can find on my <a
href="https://foundryvtt.com/community/forien/" target="_blank">Foundry Profile</a>) and
maintaining them by spending my free time. If you would like to support me and the
development of those modules, please consider <a
href="https://www.patreon.com/foundryworkshop" target="_blank"><b>becoming a Patron</b>
</a> or donating through <a href="https://www.paypal.com/cgi-bin/webscr?cmd=_s-
xclick&hosted_button_id=6P2RRX7HVEMV2&source=url" target="_blank">PayPal</a> or <a
href="https://ko-fi.com/forien" target="_blank">Ko-Fi</a></p>

**Gamemaster:** 전초기지 습격으로부터 약 반나절이 지나고…
기지의 천막들을 찢겨 있고, 바리케이드는 여전히 무너져 있습니다.
부상자는 적고 시신은 너무나 많습니다.
연기와 피 냄새가 아직 사라지지 않은 전초기지의 폐허 위, 보고를 마친 조사대장이 여러분에게
다가옵니다.

**럭키:** 열심히 시신을 수습하고 정리하는 중이다

**조사대장:** "…휴식은 하셨습니까?"

**아르시안 엘다인:** @그럼 피에스타랑 같이 왔겠군요

**피에스타:** "지옥이야.. 지옥이 따로 없다구요"

**아르시안 엘다인:** (맞다 피에스타 지금 버프 하나 걸려있는데 해제 하시면 되어오

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** 전에 있던 암살자는 사라지고 연락을 받은 사제가 도착했다."이게 다 무슨 일인가?"

**럭키:** 눈 밑이 퀭합니다

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…현재 상황에 대해 얘기 해주시겠습니까?"

**럭키:** "뭐 대충… 그렇슴다."

**라비니아:** "무시무시한 드로우들이 기지를 습격했습니다요"

**조사대장:** "방금 막 오신 분들은 상황을 잘 모르시겠군요."
"…설명을 부탁드립니다 상병."

**라비니아:** "라비니아의 엄청난 실력으로 죄다 쓰러트렸습니다요"

**럭키:** "지원임까?" 하며 새로온 면면들을 보곤 노골적으로 실망합니다
"…뉴페이스가 하나도 없잖아."
"왜 맨날 보던 맛이야?"

**피에스타:** "살아남아서 다행이라고 해줄래요?"

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…그림 할로우 이후로 전 당신을 이제야 2번 만나는겁니다만?"

**럭키:** "어쨋거나 구면이잖아. 한 번 같이 싸웠으면 이미 전우지."

**조사대장:** "수비대의 지원병력은 아직 오고있는 중입니다. 인원이 많아서 시간이 걸리는듯 싶군요."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…당신답군요. 지금까지 산게 용할 정도로 말입니다"

**피에스타:** "좀 더 빨리 구해달란 말이에요!" 도망다녔던 흔적을 탈탈 털면서 울고불고 합니다.

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…"

**럭키:** "내가 죽으면 발더스 게이트랑 오리진의 평화는 누가 지키냐."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "같은 소서러라고 해서 같이 왔습니다만은…무슨 일이 있었던겁니까?"

**라비니아:** "하퍼길드…"
"아닙니다요"

**럭키:** 라비니아의 머리에 꿀밤을 먹입니다

**라비니아:** "에에에에에에엥!!!!!"
"너무합니다요!!!"

**럭키:** "하퍼어어~? 그 지들 잘난 맛에 규율도 뭣도 없고 여기저기 쏘다니는."
"그 자칭 정의의 사도들?"

**라비니아:** "때렸습니다요!! 럭키상병님이 라비니아의 머리를 때렸습니다요!!!!"

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** "다들 그만, 그래서 해야할 일은 뭔가?"

**라비니아:** "사람의 행위가 아닙니다요!!!!"

**조사대장:** "피에스타양을 비롯한 몇몇분은 겪었다시피 드로우들의 공격을 받은 지금 전초기지는 제 기능
을 잃었습니다."

**라비니아:** "자칭이 아니라 진짜 정의의 사도들인겁니다요…!"

**조사대장:** "그래서 상부에서도 방침을 바꾼 모양이더군요."

**피에스타:** "으우으. 괜히 벌집 쑤셔놔서 그런거잖아요! 전초기지에서 쉬고 있었더니, 갑자기 막 칼든 사람
들이 와서는…"

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** "어떤 방침을 받은거지?"

**조사대장:** "해야만 하는 일이었습니다."
"조사가 아닌 전투용 부대를 보내겠다는군요."

**럭키:** "벌집 같은 소리하네. 벌들이 얼마나 좋은 생물들인데."
"까만 귀쟁이들? 해악 그 자체다."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "전투용이라…현재로서는 그게 더 좋겠군요"

**럭키:** "절멸시켜 마땅해."

**조사대장:** "소모된 인력을 대체할 지원군…"

**피에스타:** "제게는 여러분이 좀더 해악인거 같네요…"

**아르시안 엘다인:** @피에스타를 보며 "초면입니다만?"

**럭키:** "전투부대? 용병들이라도 대거 투입하나?"
"…… 또 수비대에 짬때리는거 아님까? 당신들?"

**조사대장:** "대부분 수비대 병력입니다. 하지만 문제는 그 지휘관이 가리아라는 자죠."

**피에스타:** "아. 물론.. 여러분에 몇몇 예외는 있지만.. 아무튼.."

**럭키:** 가리아에 대해 기억을 떠올려봅니다

**아르시안 엘다인:** "가리아…? 그 카이로스인가 하는 자가 아니라?"

**럭키:** 수비대 소속이면 알겠죠

**라비니아:** "가리아라는 사람은 누구입니까요?"

**Gamemaster:** 역사학 Check
🎲 1d20 - 1 = 15

**아르시안 엘다인:** "럭키 씨. 당신은 아십니까?"

**Gamemaster:** 철장막 수비대에서 유명인사. 실력은 뛰어나지만 권력의 개라는 말을 들을 정도로 귀족의 앞잡
이 노릇을 함. 수비대 내의 정치가 심화되면서 사조직을 모은다거나 하는 안좋은 소문이 들림.

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** 우선은 그들의 말을 경청하며 듣고 있습니다

**럭키:** "아… 이씨." 저절로 욕을 내뱉습니다

**아르시안 엘다인:** "반응을 보아하니 부정적인 케이스인가 보군요"

**라비니아:** "히에엑"

**조사대장:** "유명인사거든요."

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** "정확한 설명좀 부탁함세"

**라비니아:** "뭔지는 모르겠지만 럭키상병님이 저러는걸 보면"
"자기 자신의 사욕만 챙기고 시민들에게는 관심없는"

**럭키:** "됐어… 남들 앞에서 대놓고 상관 욕은 못해."

**라비니아:** "그러면서도 능력만은있어서 잘리지 않는 그런 사람인것같습니다요"
@아무말

**럭키:** 입술을 질끈 깨뭅니다. "하필 이럴 때…"

**피에스타:** "능력이 있으면 우린 이제 안전하겠네요?"

**조사대장:** "저는 그러겠지만 여러분은 아니겠죠."

**피에스타:** "그분이 오셔서 우리를 보호해주는거죠?"

**라비니아:** "히에에에에엑 역시 라비니아의 편은 없던겁니다요…!"

**아르시안 엘다인:** "뭐, 아닐거라고 예상은 했습니다만은"

**조사대장:** "아마 여러가지 구실로 험한 일을 맡는건 똑같을 겁니다."

**피에스타:** "역사학자 죽어요! 죽는다구!"

**아르시안 엘다인:** "현재로서는 수비대 병력을 여기로 다시 집결 하실 겁니까? 아니면 다른 지역으로 이동 하실겁
니까?"

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** "지금 욕만 해봤자 나아지는 것은 없네. 가능한 한 빠르게 할 일 하지."

**조사대장:** "그건…"

**럭키:** "아마 정규군은 여기랑 새 전초기지의 확보 및 수비를 맡을테고."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "한 곳에 있으면 다시 타격 받기 쉬울겁니다. 이미 적들이 진형을 알테니까요"

**럭키:** "탐험과 좀 더 공격적인 임무는 나랑 모험가들이 맡게 되겠지."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "병력이 다르다고 해서 이 지역 자체에서 유의미한 결과가 될거라고는 생각이 들지는 않는군요"

**군인:** 부상자들이 몸을 겨우 가누면서 말하는군요
"전투중에 엿들은 정보론 저분 우려대로 아직도 잔당이 꽤 남아있다고 하더군요…"
"그들의 수색대는 습격에 참여하지 않았으니 아직도 수색을 이어나가고 있을겁니다."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "흠…"

**라비니아:** "사악한 드로우는 말살!!!"

**조사대장:** "오벨리스크를 차지하기 위한 시간싸움은 아직 끝나지 않았다는 말이죠."

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** "그렇다면 수색대가 도착하기 전에 그들을 치거나 하자고."

**라비니아:** "…그치만 무섭긴합니다요…"

**아르시안 엘다인:** "제 생각이지만, 이 지역에서 더 뒤 쪽으로 후퇴를 하시는 것을 권장합니다"

**럭키:** "아님다. 사제님. 지금은 지휘관을 기다려야 함다."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "저희가 도르래로 내려온 그 넓은 통로 쪽은 어떠십니까?"

**럭키:** "우리가 떠나면 이 전초기지는 부상자들 밖에 남지 않으니 말임다."

**조사대장:** "흐음…"

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** "그렇긴 하지…"

**조사대장:** 뒤쪽에서 군화소리가 들려옵니다

**라비니아:** "히이읶"

**조사대장:** 하나 둘 정도가 아니라 수십명은 될법한 소리가요.

**럭키:** "벌써 도착한 건가? 꽤… 빠르네."

**아르시안 엘다인:** "그러게나 말입니다"

**라비니아:** "라비니아의 번개줄기가 빛나고있습니다요…!"

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** 선두에 서서 그들을 맞이할 준비를 합니다

**가리아:** 그렇게 다리를 건너온 한 기사가 불판 잔해들을 둘러보곤

**아르시안 엘다인:** "…저 분이 그 상관?"@럭키에게

**럭키:** "병력을 소집하는 데만 해도 시간이 필요할텐데… 이건 마치 나설 타이밍을 기다렸다는 듯한…
속도인걸."

**가리아:** "한심하군. 마법사 협회에서 보낸 자의 실력이 별로였나보지?"
"안그런가 모험가들?"

**럭키:** 아르시안에게 끄덕이곤 그들 앞으로 다가가서 경례합니다
"충성. 수비대의 럭키 상병임다."

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** "자네, 일을 어떻게 하는건가? 왜 이제서야 도착하는건가?"지위로 협박합니다

**아르시안 엘다인:** @럭키 쪽을 지켜봅니다
"사제. 뒤로 있으시지요. 이건 군과의 일입니다"

**가리아:** "그만. 난 너희의 상관이 될 자다."

**피에스타:** "일단은.. 이것도 기록.." 열심히 기록합니다.

**럭키:** "이미 보고받으셨겠지만 현재 부상자와 사상자가 다수 발생했슴다."
"후방으로 즉시 이동할 수 있도록 부상자는 따로 모아두었슴다. 사상자는 신원을 확인할 수 있
을만한 물건을 수집해 두었슴다."

**가리아:** "보면 안다. 이 많은 병력을 날려먹다니 아깝군. 쯧쯧쯧."

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** "그래. 누군가가 너무 늦게 도착해서 말이지."

**가리아:** "늦어? 우리는 너희의 사후보고를 받고 똥을 치우러 온 사람이란 말이다."
"같은 귀족으로서 그 이상의 발언은 모욕으로 간주하지."

**라비니아:** @작게 소근거립니다
"어마어마한 대머리입니다요 욕망이 머리까지 차올라서 머리카락들이 도망쳐버린겁니다요…"

**가리아:** "…잠깐 품위없는 말을 내뱉었군."

**아르시안 엘다인:** @발레리를 쳐다보다가 "가리아 상관이라고 하셨습니까? 그럼 병력은 어느정도 오셨고 현재 전
력을 어떻게 하실지 궁금합니다만 얘기해주시겠습니까?"

**피에스타:** 분위기가 험악하면 눈치를 봅니다.

**가리아:** 옷차림을 정돈하곤 질문에 답합니다.

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** 우선은 화를 가라앉힙니다

**가리아:** "병력은 약 쉰. 내 휘하의 정예들로 구성되었다."

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** 저런 것은 나중에 처리할 예정이겠군요

**가리아:** "나는 이곳을 재건하고 드로우 잔당들을 소탕하는데 집중하려고 한다."

**조사대장:** "드로우 소탕이라니? 보고에 은둔한 마법사에 대한 내용을 잊어먹기라도 한 겁니까?!"

**가리아:** "조용히 해라. 모든건 상부의 뜻이다."

**아르시안 엘다인:** @조사대장과 가리아를 번갈아 보다가 생각 합니다. 혹시 정치적인 일에 엮여져있는지

**가리아:** 그러면서 의원의 직인이 찍힌 명령서를 보여주는군요.

**라비니아:** (깝치면 안된다…!

**럭키:** "지휘관님? 별동대에도 추가 인력으로 새 모험가들이 도착했습니다. 그들은 임무를 기다리고 있

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** Star Map of Creation
This scroll displays what the night sky looked like at the creation of the
Mundane World. If you have proficiency with the Arcana or Nature skill, you can
spend 1 minute holding and studying the map and search it for an omen about
the results of a specific course of action that you plan to take within the next 30
minutes. The GM chooses from the following possible outcomes:

**Good omen:** Bad omen
Mixed omen that has both good and bad results
No omen for a result that isn’t especially good or bad
The omen doesn’t take into account any possible circumstances that might
change the outcome, such as the loss or gain of equipment or a companion.
If the map is used two or more times in 24 hours, there is a cumulative 25
percent chance for each reading after the first that you get a random reading.
The GM makes this roll in secret.

**Finger Guns:** You extend your forefinger and thumb, a dangerous gesture mimicking a gun.
For the duration, your hand counts as a Simple Ranged weapon with a range of
60/240 feet and the Slow mastery property. You can use your spellcasting ability
instead of Dexterity for the attack rolls of this weapon. On a hit, the weapon
deals 2d6 Force damage and doesn’t add your ability modifier to damage.
Cantrip Upgrade. The weapon’s normal range increases by 30 feet and its long
range increases by 120 feet when you reach levels 5 (90/360 feet), 11 (120/480
feet), and 17 (150/600 feet).

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** At Your Side
You and up to three other willing creatures of your choice within range form an
arcane bond, which magically pulls you forward when moving towards each
other. For the duration, each target’s speed increases by 5 feet, and whenever
an affected creature ends its turn, other targets of the spell can use their
reaction to move up to half their speed in the direction of another affected
creature.
At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 3rd level or
higher, you can target one additional creature for each slot level above 2nd.

The ground in a 20-foot-radius Sphere centered on a point within range sprouts
hard spikes and thorns. The area becomes Difficult Terrain for the duration.
When a creature moves into or within the area, it takes 2d4 Piercing damage for
every 5 feet it travels.
The transformation of the ground is camouflaged to look natural. Any creature
that can’t see the area when the spell is cast must take a Search action and
succeed on a Wisdom (Perception or Survival) check against your spell save DC
to recognize the terrain as hazardous before entering it.

**Controlled Mutation:** When you cast this spell, you gain 1 Contamination Level.
You weave contaminated energy to temporarily imbue a creature within range
with a beneficial mutation. Choose one of the following effects; the target gains
that effect until the spell ends.
Strength.The target has advantage on Strength attack rolls, ability checks, and
saving throws. The target can choose to gain a Contamination Level. If it does,
its melee weapon attacks deal an additional 2d6 necrotic damage for the spell’s
duration.
Constitution. The target has advantage on Constitution checks and saving
throws. The target can choose to gain a Contamination Level. If it does, it gains
resistance to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing damage for the spell’s
duration.
Dexterity. The target has advantage on Dexterity attack rolls, ability checks, and
saving throws. The target can choose to gain a Contamination Level. If it does,
its attacks with ranged and finesse weapons score a critical hit on an 18–20 for
the spell’s duration.
Intelligence. The target has advantage on Intelligence ability checks and saving
throws, as well as spell attack rolls. The target can also choose to gain a
Contamination Level. If it does, for the duration of this spell, while the target is
concentrating on a spell it has cast, it’s concentration can’t be broken as a
result of taking damage.
Wisdom. The target has advantage on Wisdom ability checks and saving
throws, as well as spell attack rolls. The target can also choose to gain a
Contamination Level. If it does, for the duration of this spell, it gains blindsight
to a range of 60 feet and can’t be surprised while it is conscious.
Charisma.The target has advantage on Charisma ability checks and saving
throws, as well as spell attack rolls. In addition, the target can choose to gain a
Contamination Level. If it does, for the duration of this spell, when the target
makes a Charisma (Persuasion) or Charisma (Deception) check, it can treat a
d20 roll of 9 or lower as a 10.
At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 3rd level or
higher, you can choose one additional effect for every two slot levels above
2nd.

**Innate Sorcery:** An event in your past left an indelible mark on you, infusing you with simmering
magic. As a Bonus Action, you can unleash that magic for 1 minute, during
which you gain the following benefits:
The spell save DC of your Sorcerer spells increases by 1.
You have Advantage on the attack rolls of Sorcerer spells you cast.
You can use this feature twice, and you regain all expended uses of it when you
finish a Long Rest.

You extend your forefinger and thumb, a dangerous gesture mimicking a gun.
For the duration, your hand counts as a Simple Ranged weapon with a range of
60/240 feet and the Slow mastery property. You can use your spellcasting ability
instead of Dexterity for the attack rolls of this weapon. On a hit, the weapon
deals 2d6 Force damage and doesn’t add your ability modifier to damage.
Cantrip Upgrade. The weapon’s normal range increases by 30 feet and its long
range increases by 120 feet when you reach levels 5 (90/360 feet), 11 (120/480
feet), and 17 (150/600 feet).

이 볼 수 있는 지정된 목표에게 날아가 명중합니다. 각각의 다트는 1d4 +1 역장 피해를 가합
니다. 다트는 모두 동시에 타격을 가하며, 하나의 목표에 다트를 모두 쏘거나 여러 목표에게
나누어 쏠 수 있습니다.

레벨 하나당 추가로 다트를 하나 더 생성하여 발사할 수 있습니다.

문이 있다면 주문 각각에 대해 당신의 주문시전 능력치를 사용해 능력 판정을 행합니다. 이때
판정의 DC는 10 + 대상 주문의 레벨입니다. 판정에 성공한 경우, 해당 주문 역시 종료됩니
다.

**Wrath of the Sea:** As a Bonus Action, you can expend a use of your Wild Shape to manifest a 5-
foot Emanation that takes the form of ocean spray that surrounds you for 10
minutes. It ends early if you dismiss it (no action required), manifest it again, or
have the Incapacitated condition.
When you manifest the Emanation and as a Bonus Action on your subsequent
turns, you can choose another creature you can see in the Emanation. The
target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your spell save DC
or take Cold damage and, if the creature is Large or smaller, be pushed up to 15
feet away from you. To determine this damage, roll a number of d6s equal to
your Wisdom modifier (minimum of one die).

**Startling Speed:** Your movements are so swift that you are almost invisible when in motion. If
you move at least 10 feet on your turn, attack rolls against you have
disadvantage until the start of your next turn. This feature does not function if
you are incapacitated or restrained. You can use this ability a number of rounds
per day equal to your level.

You magically mark one creature you can see within range as your quarry. Until
the spell ends, you deal an extra 1d6 Force damage to the target whenever you
hit it with an attack roll. You also have Advantage on any 지혜 (감지) or 지혜 (생존
술) check you make to find it.
If the target drops to 0 Hit Points before this spell ends, you can take a Bonus
Action to move the mark to a new creature you can see within range.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. Your Concentration can last longer with a spell
slot of level 3–4 (up to 8 hours) or 5+ (up to 24 hours).

당신은 마법의 힘으로 빛나는 3개의 다트를 만들어 냅니다. 각각의 다트는 사거리 내의, 당신
이 볼 수 있는 지정된 목표에게 날아가 명중합니다. 각각의 다트는 1d4 +1 역장 피해를 가합
니다. 다트는 모두 동시에 타격을 가하며, 하나의 목표에 다트를 모두 쏘거나 여러 목표에게
나누어 쏠 수 있습니다.
상위시전. 당신이 2레벨 이상의 주문 슬롯을 사용하여 이 주문을 시전할 경우, 상승한 슬롯
레벨 하나당 추가로 다트를 하나 더 생성하여 발사할 수 있습니다.
🎲 1d4 + 1 = 5

With a boom that can be heard 300 feet away (or 1,000 feet in a liquid), a pulse
of thunder ripples out from a point you choose within range. Each creature in a
20-foot-radius sphere centred on that point must make a Constitution saving
throw. A target takes 7d6 thunder damage on a failed save, or half as much
damage on a successful one. This damage increases to 9d6 if the affected
creature is submerged in a liquid.
At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 4th level or
higher, the damage increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 3rd.

**드로우 견습 마술사:** 인간형 포박
당신은 사거리 내에 자신이 볼 수 있는 인간형 크리처 하나를 지정합니다. 이렇게 지정된 목
표는 지혜 내성 굴림을 굴려야 하며, 실패할 시 주문의 지속시간 동안 마비 상태가 됩니다. 목
표는 자기 턴이 끝날 때마다 다시 지혜 내성 굴림을 굴릴 수 있으며, 성공할 경우 목표는 주문
에서 벗어날 수 있습니다.
상위시전. 당신이 3레벨 이상의 주문 슬롯을 사용해서 이 주문을 사용할 경우, 상승한 주문
슬롯 레벨 하나당 추가적으로 인간형 대상을 하나씩 더 지정할 수 있습니다. 각각의 목표는
서로 30ft 내에 모여 있어야 합니다.

Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d6 when you reach levels 5 (2d6),
11 (3d6), and 17 (4d6).

You magically mark one creature you can see within range as your quarry. Until
the spell ends, you deal an extra 1d6 Force damage to the target whenever you
hit it with an attack roll. You also have Advantage on any 지혜 (감지) or 지혜 (생존
술) check you make to find it.
If the target drops to 0 Hit Points before this spell ends, you can take a Bonus
Action to move the mark to a new creature you can see within range.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. Your Concentration can last longer with a spell
slot of level 3–4 (up to 8 hours) or 5+ (up to 24 hours).

**라비니아:** Ominous Winds
Up to three creatures of your choice that you can see within range must make
Charisma saving throws. Whenever a target that fails this saving throw makes
an attack roll or a saving throw before the spell ends, the target must roll a
1d12 and subtract the number rolled from the attack roll or saving throw.
At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 3rd level or
higher, you can target one additional creature for each slot level above 2nd.

**드로우 마검사:** Counterspell
You attempt to interrupt a creature in the process of casting a spell. The
creature makes a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, the spell
dissipates with no effect, and the action, Bonus Action, or Reaction used to cast
it is wasted. If that spell was cast with a spell slot, the slot isn't expended.

**럭키:** Stunning Strike
Once per turn when you hit a creature with a Monk weapon or an Unarmed
Strike, you can expend 1 Focus Point to attempt a stunning strike. The target
must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, the target has the
Stunned condition until the start of your next turn. On a successful save, the
target’s Speed is halved until the start of your next turn, and the next attack roll
made against the target before then has Advantage.

**라비니아:** Unarmed Strike
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**드로우 전사:** 민첩 내성 굴림13 🎲 1d20 + 4 + 3 + 0 = 13

**라비니아:** 잡혀랏

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Mage Hand:** A spectral, floating hand appears at a point you choose within range. The hand
lasts for the duration. The hand vanishes if it is ever more than 30 feet away
from you or if you cast this spell again.
When you cast the spell, you can use the hand to manipulate an object, open
an unlocked door or container, stow or retrieve an item from an open container,
or pour the contents out of a vial.
As a Magic action on your later turns, you can control the hand thus again. As
part of that action, you can move the hand up to 30 feet.
The hand can’t attack, activate magic items, or carry more than 10 pounds.

**Thaumaturgy:** You manifest a minor wonder within range. You create one of the effects below
within range. If you cast this spell multiple times, you can have up to three of its
1-minute effects active at a time.
Altered Eyes. You alter the appearance of your eyes for 1 minute.
Booming Voice. Your voice booms up to three times as loud as normal for 1
minute. For the duration, you have Advantage on Charisma (Intimidation)
checks.
Fire Play. You cause flames to flicker, brighten, dim, or change color for 1
minute.
Invisible Hand. You instantaneously cause an unlocked door or window to fly
open or slam shut.
Phantom Sound. You create an instantaneous sound that originates from a
point of your choice within range, such as a rumble of thunder, the cry of a
raven, or ominous whispers.
Tremors. You cause harmless tremors in the ground for 1 minute.

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** Moment to Think
When you cast this spell, you briefly stop time for everyone but yourself. You
can take one additional action and move around in your space while no time
passes for other creatures. That action can be used only to take the Search,
Study, or Utilize action. Furthermore, you can’t affect or damage any creature or
object, other than objects you are wearing or carrying. If an object leaves your
hand, it also becomes frozen in time.

You magically distract the triggering creature and turn its momentary
uncertainty into encouragement for another creature. The triggering creature
must reroll the d20 and use the lower roll.
You can then choose a different creature you can see within range (you can
choose yourself). The chosen creature has advantage on the next attack roll,
ability check, or saving throw it makes within 1 minute. A creature can be
empowered by only one use of this spell at a time.

**라비니아:** Spike Growth
The ground in a 20-foot-radius Sphere centered on a point within range sprouts
hard spikes and thorns. The area becomes Difficult Terrain for the duration.
When a creature moves into or within the area, it takes 2d4 Piercing damage for
every 5 feet it travels.
The transformation of the ground is camouflaged to look natural. Any creature
that can’t see the area when the spell is cast must take a Search action and
succeed on a Wisdom (Perception or Survival) check against your spell save DC
to recognize the terrain as hazardous before entering it.

**라비니아:** Wrath of the Sea
As a Bonus Action, you can expend a use of your Wild Shape to manifest a 5-
foot Emanation that takes the form of ocean spray that surrounds you for 10
minutes. It ends early if you dismiss it (no action required), manifest it again, or
have the Incapacitated condition.
When you manifest the Emanation and as a Bonus Action on your subsequent
turns, you can choose another creature you can see in the Emanation. The
target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your spell save DC
or take Cold damage and, if the creature is Large or smaller, be pushed up to 15
feet away from you. To determine this damage, roll a number of d6s equal to
your Wisdom modifier (minimum of one die).

Metamagic: Quickened Spell
Cost: 2 Sorcery Points
When you cast a spell that has a casting time of an action, you can spend 2
Sorcery Points to change the casting time to a Bonus Action for this casting. You
can’t modify a spell in this way if you’ve already cast a level 1+ spell on the
current turn, nor can you cast a level 1+ spell on this turn after modifying a
spell in this way.

For the duration, an inky aura surrounds one creature you touch. The target has
Advantage on Death Saving Throws, and once per turn, when a creature within
5 feet of the target hits it with a melee attack roll, the attacker takes 2d4
Necrotic damage.

**아르시안 엘다인:** Bless
You bless up to three creatures within range. Whenever a target makes an attack
roll or a saving throw before the spell ends, the target adds 1d4 to the attack
roll or save.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. You can target one additional creature for
each spell slot level above 1.

**아르시안 엘다인:** Restore Balance
Your connection to the plane of absolute order allows you to equalize chaotic
moments. When a creature you can see within 60 feet of yourself is about to roll
a d20 with Advantage or Disadvantage, you can take a Reaction to prevent the
roll from being affected by Advantage and Disadvantage.
You can use this feature a number of times equal to your Charisma modifier
(minimum of once), and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long
Rest.

**라비니아:** 오

**아르시안 엘다인:** 불리를 일반으로 상쇄합니다

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** Fire Bolt
You hurl a mote of fire at a creature or an object within range. Make a ranged
spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d10 Fire damage. A
flammable object hit by this spell starts burning if it isn’t being worn or carried.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d10 when you reach levels 5
(2d10), 11 (3d10), and 17 (4d10).
🎲 1d20 + 3 + 2 + 1d4 = 11

**키메라:** 그럼 일반으로 치면 됨다

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** Invoke Duplicity
As a Bonus Action, you can expend one use of your Channel Divinity to create a
perfect visual illusion of yourself in an unoccupied space you can see within 30
feet of yourself. The illusion is intangible and doesn’t occupy its space. It lasts
for 1 minute, but it ends early if you dismiss it (no action required) or have the
Incapacitated condition. The illusion is animated and mimics your expressions
and gestures. While it persists, you gain the following benefits.
Cast Spells. You can cast spells as though you were in the illusion’s space, but
you must use your own senses.
Distract. When both you and your illusion are within 5 feet of a creature that
can see the illusion, you have Advantage on attack rolls against that creature,
given how distracting the illusion is to the target.
Move. As a Bonus Action, you can move the illusion up to 30 feet to an
unoccupied space you can see that is within 120 feet of yourself.

**라비니아:** Spike Growth
The ground in a 20-foot-radius Sphere centered on a point within range sprouts
hard spikes and thorns. The area becomes Difficult Terrain for the duration.
When a creature moves into or within the area, it takes 2d4 Piercing damage for
every 5 feet it travels.
The transformation of the ground is camouflaged to look natural. Any creature
that can’t see the area when the spell is cast must take a Search action and
succeed on a Wisdom (Perception or Survival) check against your spell save DC
to recognize the terrain as hazardous before entering it.
🎲 2d4 = 7

**피에스타:** Innate Sorcery
An event in your past left an indelible mark on you, infusing you with simmering
magic. As a Bonus Action, you can unleash that magic for 1 minute, during
which you gain the following benefits:
The spell save DC of your Sorcerer spells increases by 1.
You have Advantage on the attack rolls of Sorcerer spells you cast.
You can use this feature twice, and you regain all expended uses of it when you
finish a Long Rest.

**라비니아:** Water Bullet
You create a sphere of swirling water that spins rapidly in your hand or mouth
before you hurl it at a creature within range. Make a ranged spell attack against
the target. On a hit, the target takes bludgeoning damage based on how far it is
away from you.
1–10 feet: 5d6
11–60 feet: 4d6
61–90 feet: 3d6
At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 2nd level or
higher, the damage increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 1st.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 = 21
🎲 5d6 = 18

An event in your past left an indelible mark on you, infusing you with simmering
magic. As a Bonus Action, you can unleash that magic for 1 minute, during
which you gain the following benefits:
The spell save DC of your Sorcerer spells increases by 1.
You have Advantage on the attack rolls of Sorcerer spells you cast.
You can use this feature twice, and you regain all expended uses of it when you
finish a Long Rest.

**아르시안 엘다인:** Finger Guns
You extend your forefinger and thumb, a dangerous gesture mimicking a gun.
For the duration, your hand counts as a Simple Ranged weapon with a range of
60/240 feet and the Slow mastery property. You can use your spellcasting ability
instead of Dexterity for the attack rolls of this weapon. On a hit, the weapon
deals 2d6 Force damage and doesn’t add your ability modifier to damage.
Cantrip Upgrade. The weapon’s normal range increases by 30 feet and its long
range increases by 120 feet when you reach levels 5 (90/360 feet), 11 (120/480
feet), and 17 (150/600 feet).

Your connection to the plane of absolute order allows you to equalize chaotic
moments. When a creature you can see within 60 feet of yourself is about to roll
a d20 with Advantage or Disadvantage, you can take a Reaction to prevent the
roll from being affected by Advantage and Disadvantage.
You can use this feature a number of times equal to your Charisma modifier
(minimum of once), and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long
Rest.

You unleash a wave of thunderous energy. Each creature in a 15-foot Cube
originating from you makes a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, a
creature takes 2d8 Thunder damage and is pushed 10 feet away from you. On a
successful save, a creature takes half as much damage only.
In addition, unsecured objects that are entirely within the Cube are pushed 10
feet away from you, and a thunderous boom is audible within 300 feet.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The damage increases by 1d8 for each spell
slot level above 1.

you are incapacitated or restrained. You can use this ability a number of rounds

For the duration, your hand counts as a Simple Ranged weapon with a range of
60/240 feet and the Slow mastery property. You can use your spellcasting ability
instead of Dexterity for the attack rolls of this weapon. On a hit, the weapon

range increases by 120 feet when you reach levels 5 (90/360 feet), 11 (120/480
feet), and 17 (150/600 feet).

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** Unarmed Strike
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.
🎲 1d20 - 1 + 2 + 1d4 = 14

**Ball Bearings:** As a Utilize action, you can spill Ball Bearings from their pouch. They spread to
cover a level, 10-foot-square area within 10 feet of yourself. A creature that
enters this area for the first time on a turn must succeed on a DC 10 Dexterity
saving throw or have the Prone condition. It takes 10 minutes to recover the
Ball Bearings.

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** Spiritual Weapon
You create a floating, spectral force that resembles a weapon of your choice and
lasts for the duration. The force appears within range in a space of your choice,
and you can immediately make one melee spell attack against one creature
within 5 feet of the force. On a hit, the target takes Force damage equal to 1d8
plus your spellcasting ability modifier.
As a Bonus Action on your later turns, you can move the force up to 20 feet and
repeat the attack against a creature within 5 feet of it.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The damage increases by 1d8 for every slot
level above 2.

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** Spiritual Weapon
You create a floating, spectral force that resembles a weapon of your choice and
lasts for the duration. The force appears within range in a space of your choice,
and you can immediately make one melee spell attack against one creature
within 5 feet of the force. On a hit, the target takes Force damage equal to 1d8
plus your spellcasting ability modifier.
As a Bonus Action on your later turns, you can move the force up to 20 feet and
repeat the attack against a creature within 5 feet of it.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The damage increases by 1d8 for every slot
level above 2.

**쭉정이의 턴:** Regeneration
The limb regains 5 Hit Points at the start of each of its turns. If the limb takes
Acid or Fire damage, this trait doesn’t function on the limb’s next turn. The limb
dies only if it starts its turn with 0 Hit Points and doesn’t regenerate.

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** Oil
You can douse a creature, object, or space with Oil or use it as fuel, as detailed
below.
Dousing a Creature or an Object. When you take the Attack action, you can
replace one of your attacks with throwing an Oil flask. Target one creature or
object within 20 feet of yourself. The target must succeed on a Dexterity saving
throw (DC 8 plus your Dexterity modifier and Proficiency Bonus) or be covered
in oil. If the target takes Fire damage before the oil dries (after 1 minute), the
target takes an extra 5 Fire damage from burning oil.
Dousing a Space. You can take the Utilize action to pour an Oil flask on level
ground to cover a 5-foot-square area within 5 feet of yourself. If lit, the oil burns
until the end of the turn 2 rounds from when the oil was lit (or 12 seconds) and
deals 5 Fire damage to any creature that enters the area or ends its turn there. A
creature can take this damage only once per turn.
Fuel. Oil serves as fuel for Lamps and Lanterns. Once lit, a flask of Oil burns for
6 hours in a Lamp or Lantern. That duration doesn’t need to be consecutive;
you can extinguish the burning Oil (as a Utilize action) and rekindle it again
until it has burned for a total of 6 hours.

**Moment to Think:** When you cast this spell, you briefly stop time for everyone but yourself. You
can take one additional action and move around in your space while no time
passes for other creatures. That action can be used only to take the Search,
Study, or Utilize action. Furthermore, you can’t affect or damage any creature or
object, other than objects you are wearing or carrying. If an object leaves your
hand, it also becomes frozen in time.

**라비니아:** Create Bonfire
You create a bonfire on ground that you can see within range. Until the spell
ends, the magic bonfire fills a 5-foot cube. Any creature in the bonfire’s space
when you cast the spell must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or take 1d8
fire damage. A creature must also make the saving throw when it moves into
the bonfire’s space for the first time on a turn or ends its turn there.
The bonfire ignites flammable objects in its area that aren’t being worn or
carried.
The spell’s damage increases by 1d8 when you reach 5th level (2d8), 11th level
(3d8), and 17th level (4d8).
🎲 2d8 = 7

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** Fire Bolt
You hurl a mote of fire at a creature or an object within range. Make a ranged
spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d10 Fire damage. A
flammable object hit by this spell starts burning if it isn’t being worn or carried.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d10 when you reach levels 5
(2d10), 11 (3d10), and 17 (4d10).
🎲 1d20 + 3 + 2 = 23
🎲 1d10 = 3
